(**************************************************************************************************

  Right actions of a monoid

  For any monoid M, there is a category of sets with a right M-action. This file defines the objects
  and morphisms in this category, defines the category itself, and shows that it has a terminal
  object, binary products and exponentials. Also, a morphism between two monoids induces
  "restriction" and "extension" of scalar functors between their categories of monoid actions. The
  extension functor preserves the terminal object and binary product.

  Contents
  1.  The category of monoid action data and its objects
    [monoid_action_data_cat] [monoid_action_data]
  2.  The category of monoid actions [monoid_action_cat]
  3.  The definition of a right M-action [monoid_action]
  4.  The definition of a morphism of M-actions [monoid_action_morphism]
  5.  The terminal M-action [terminal_monoid_action]
  6.  The binary product of M-actions [binproducts_monoid_action_cat]
  7.  The exponential M-action [is_exponentiable_monoid_action]
  8.  A characterization of isomorphisms [make_monoid_action_z_iso]
  9.  An isomorphism between the set of global elements and the set of fixpoints of a monoid action [monoid_action_global_element_fixpoint_iso]
  10.  Restriction of scalars [scalar_restriction_functor]
  11. Extension of scalars [scalar_extension_functor]
  11.1. Extension of scalars preserves monoid monoid action
    [scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action]
  11.2. Extension of scalars preserves the terminal [scalar_extension_preserves_terminal]
  11.3. Extension of scalars preserves binary products [scalar_extension_preserves_binproducts]

 **************************************************************************************************)

(** * 1. The category of monoid action data and its objects *)

  Definition action_ax
    (X : hSet)
    (x : X)
    (m : M)
    : UU
    := X.

  Let mor_action_ax'
    {X X' : hSet}
    (action : ∏ x m, action_ax X x m)
    (action' : ∏ x m, action_ax X' x m)
    (f : X → X')
    (x : X)
    (m : M)
    : UU
    := f (action x m) = action' (f x) m.

(action : ∏ (x : X)

           (m : M), 
           action_ax X' x m)

f (action x m) = action' (f x) m: ∏ X X' : hSet,
(∏ (x : X) (m : M), action_ax X x m)
→ (∏ (x : X') (m : M),
   action_ax X' x m)
  → (X → X') → X → M → UU
disp_cat SET

M: monoid
mor_action_ax':= λ (X X' : hSet)
(action : ∏ (x : X) 
          (m : M), action_ax X x m)
(action' : ∏ (x : X') 
           (m : M), 
           action_ax X' x m)
(f : X → X') (x : X) 
(m : M),

(∏ (x : X) (m : M), action_ax X x m)
→ (∏ (x : X') (m : M),
   action_ax X' x m)
  → (X → X') → X → M → UU
∏ (x y z : SET)
(a : (λ X : SET, ∏ (x0 : X) (m : M), action_ax X x0 m)
       x)
(b : (λ X : SET, ∏ (x0 : X) (m : M), action_ax X x0 m)
       y)
(c : (λ X : SET, ∏ (x0 : X) (m : M), action_ax X x0 m)
       z) (f : SET ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : SET ⟦ y, z ⟧),
(λ (X X' : SET)
 (action : (λ X0 : SET,
            ∏ (x0 : X0) (m : M), action_ax X0 x0 m) X)
 (action' : (λ X0 : SET,
             ∏ (x0 : X0) (m : M), action_ax X0 x0 m)
              X') (f0 : SET ⟦ X, X' ⟧),
 ∏ (x0 : X) (m : M),
 mor_action_ax' action action' f0 x0 m) x y a b f
→ (λ (X X' : SET)
   (action : (λ X0 : SET,
              ∏ (x0 : X0) (m : M), action_ax X0 x0 m)
               X)
   (action' : (λ X0 : SET,
               ∏ (x0 : X0) (m : M), action_ax X0 x0 m)
                X') (f0 : SET ⟦ X, X' ⟧),
   ∏ (x0 : X) (m : M),
   mor_action_ax' action action' f0 x0 m) y z b c g
  → (λ (X X' : SET)
     (action : (λ X0 : SET,
                ∏ (x0 : X0) (m : M), action_ax X0 x0 m)
                 X)
     (action' : (λ X0 : SET,
                 ∏ (x0 : X0) (m : M),
                 action_ax X0 x0 m) X')
     (f0 : SET ⟦ X, X' ⟧),
     ∏ (x0 : X) (m : M),
     mor_action_ax' action action' f0 x0 m) x z a c
      (f · g)
 abstract (
        intros X X' X'' action action' action'' f g f_action g_action x m;
        exact (maponpaths _ (f_action _ _) @ g_action _ _)
      ).
  Defined.

  Definition monoid_action_data_cat
    : category
    := total_category monoid_action_data_disp_cat.

  Definition monoid_action_data : UU
    := monoid_action_data_cat.

  Definition make_monoid_action_data
    (X : hSet)
    (action : X → M → X)
    : monoid_action_data
    := X ,, action.

End DataCat.

Arguments action_ax /.

Coercion monoid_action_data_to_hset {M : monoid} (x : monoid_action_data M) : hSet := pr1 x.

Definition action
  {M : monoid}
  {X : monoid_action_data M}
  (x : X)
  (m : M)
  : action_ax M X x m
  := pr2 X x m.

(** * 2. The category of monoid actions *)

Definition action_unel_ax
  {M : monoid}
  (X : monoid_action_data M)
  (x : X)
  : UU
  := action x 1 = x.

Arguments action_unel_ax /.

Definition action_op_ax
  {M : monoid}
  (X : monoid_action_data M)
  (x : X)
  (m m' : M)
  : UU
  := action x (m * m') = action (action x m) m'.

Arguments action_op_ax /.

Definition is_monoid_action
  {M : monoid}
  (X : monoid_action_data M)
  : UU
  := (∏ x, action_unel_ax X x)
    × (∏ x m m', action_op_ax X x m m').

Definition monoid_action_cat
  (M : monoid)
  : category
  := full_subcat (monoid_action_data_cat M) is_monoid_action.

(** * 3. The definition of a right M-action *)

Definition monoid_action
  (M : monoid)
  : UU
  := monoid_action_cat M.

Definition make_is_monoid_action
  {M : monoid}
  {X : monoid_action_data M}
  (action_unel : ∏ x, action_unel_ax X x)
  (action_op : ∏ x m m', action_op_ax X x m m')
  : is_monoid_action X
  := action_unel ,, action_op.

Definition make_monoid_action
  {M : monoid}
  (X : monoid_action_data M)
  (H : is_monoid_action X)
  : monoid_action M
  := X ,, H.

Coercion monoid_action_to_monoid_action_data
  (M : monoid)
  (f : monoid_action M)
  : monoid_action_data M
  := pr1 f.

Definition action_unel
  {M : monoid}
  (X : monoid_action M)
  (x : X)
  : action_unel_ax X x
  := pr12 X x.

Definition action_op
  {M : monoid}
  (X : monoid_action M)
  (x : X)
  (m m' : M)
  : action_op_ax X x m m'
  := pr22 X x m m'.


M: monoid
X: monoid_action_data M
isaprop (is_monoid_action X)

isaprop (is_monoid_action X)

  apply isapropdirprod;
    repeat (apply impred_isaprop; intro);
    apply setproperty.
Qed.

    ).
Defined.

(** * 4. The definition of a morphism of M-actions *)

Definition mor_action_ax
  {M : monoid}
  {X X' : monoid_action M}
  (f : X → X')
  (x : X)
  (m : M)
  : UU
  := f (action x m) = action (f x) m.

Arguments mor_action_ax /.

Definition monoid_action_morphism
  {M : monoid}
  (X X' : monoid_action M)
  : UU
  := monoid_action_cat M⟦X, X'⟧.

Definition make_monoid_action_morphism
  {M : monoid}
  {X X' : monoid_action M}
  (f : X → X')
  (H : ∏ x m, mor_action_ax f x m)
  : monoid_action_morphism X X'
  := (f ,, H) ,, tt.

Definition monoid_action_morphism_to_function
  {M : monoid}
  {X X' : monoid_action M}
  (f : monoid_action_morphism X X')
  : X → X'
  := pr11 f.

Coercion monoid_action_morphism_to_function: monoid_action_morphism >-> Funclass.

Definition mor_action
  {M : monoid}
  {X X' : monoid_action M}
  (f : monoid_action_morphism X X')
  (x : X)
  (m : M)
  : mor_action_ax f x m
  := pr21 f x m.

Definition binproducts_monoid_action_cat
  (M : monoid)
  : BinProducts (monoid_action_cat M)
  := binproduct_monoid_action_cat.

(** * 7. The exponential M-action *)

Section ExponentialObject.

  Context {M : monoid}.
  Context (X X' : monoid_action M).

  Let binproduct_monoid_action
    (Y Y' : monoid_action M)
    : monoid_action M
    := BinProductObject _ (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M Y Y').

  Section ActionOnMorphism.

    Context (f : monoid_action_morphism (binproduct_monoid_action (monoid_monoid_action M) X) X').
    Context (m : M).

    Definition action_on_morphism_data
      : binproduct_monoid_action (monoid_monoid_action M) X → X'
      := λ x, f (m * pr1 x ,, pr2 x).

    
M: monoid
X, X': monoid_action M
binproduct_monoid_action:= λ Y Y' : monoid_action M,
binproducts_monoid_action_cat
  M Y Y': monoid_action M
→ monoid_action M
  → monoid_action M
f: monoid_action_morphism
  (binproduct_monoid_action
     (monoid_monoid_action M) X) X'
m: M
∏
(x : binproduct_monoid_action (monoid_monoid_action M)
       X) (m : M),
mor_action_ax action_on_morphism_data x m

    
M: monoid
X, X': monoid_action M
binproduct_monoid_action:= λ Y Y' : monoid_action M,
binproducts_monoid_action_cat
  M Y Y': monoid_action M
→ monoid_action M
  → monoid_action M

  (binproduct_monoid_action
     (monoid_monoid_action M) X) X'
m: M
∏
(x : binproduct_monoid_action (monoid_monoid_action M)
       X) (m : M),
mor_action_ax action_on_morphism_data x m

      
M: monoid
X, X': monoid_action M
binproduct_monoid_action:= λ Y Y' : monoid_action M,
binproducts_monoid_action_cat
  M Y Y': monoid_action M
→ monoid_action M
  → monoid_action M
f: monoid_action_morphism
  (binproduct_monoid_action
     (monoid_monoid_action M) X) X'
m: M
x: binproduct_monoid_action 
  (monoid_monoid_action M) X
m': M
mor_action_ax action_on_morphism_data x m'

      
M: monoid
X, X': monoid_action M
binproduct_monoid_action:= λ Y Y' : monoid_action M,
binproducts_monoid_action_cat
  M Y Y': monoid_action M
→ monoid_action M
  → monoid_action M
f: monoid_action_morphism
  (binproduct_monoid_action
     (monoid_monoid_action M) X) X'
m: M
x: binproduct_monoid_action 
  (monoid_monoid_action M) X
m': M
action_on_morphism_data (action x m') =
f (action ((m + pr1 x)%addmonoid,, pr2 x) m')

      exact (maponpaths (λ x, f (x ,, _)) (!assocax M _ _ _)).
    Qed.

    Definition action_on_morphism
      : monoid_action_morphism (binproduct_monoid_action (monoid_monoid_action M) X) X'
      := make_monoid_action_morphism _ action_on_morphism_is_morphism.

  End ActionOnMorphism.

  → monoid_action M
monoid_action_data M

  Definition exponential_object
    : monoid_action M
    := make_monoid_action _ exponential_is_object.

  Definition exponential_object_morphism_data
    : binproduct_monoid_action X exponential_object → X'
    := λ x, (pr2 x : monoid_action_morphism _ _) (1 ,, pr1 x).

x: restriction_functor_ob_monoid_action X
m: M
mor_action_ax
  restriction_functor_mor_monoid_action_morphism_data
  x m

      apply (mor_action F).
    Qed.

    Definition restriction_functor_mor_monoid_action_morphism
      : monoid_action_morphism
        (restriction_functor_ob_monoid_action X)
        (restriction_functor_ob_monoid_action X')
      := make_monoid_action_morphism _ restriction_functor_mor_is_monoid_action_morphism.

  End Mor.

  Definition scalar_restriction_functor_data
    : functor_data (monoid_action_cat M') (monoid_action_cat M)
    := make_functor_data (C := monoid_action_cat M') (C' := monoid_action_cat M)
      restriction_functor_ob_monoid_action
      restriction_functor_mor_monoid_action_morphism.

# scalar_restriction_functor_data (identity X) =
identity (scalar_restriction_functor_data X)

f: monoidfun M M'
X: monoid_action_cat M'
∏ x : scalar_restriction_functor_data X,
# scalar_restriction_functor_data (identity X) x =
identity (scalar_restriction_functor_data X) x

      easy.
    
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
functor_compax scalar_restriction_functor_data
 
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'

F'': monoid_action_cat M' ⟦ X', X'' ⟧
# scalar_restriction_functor_data (F · F'') =
# scalar_restriction_functor_data F
· # scalar_restriction_functor_data F''

      
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
X, X', X'': monoid_action_cat M'

∏ x : scalar_restriction_functor_data X,
# scalar_restriction_functor_data (F · F'') x =
(# scalar_restriction_functor_data F
 · # scalar_restriction_functor_data F'') x

      easy.
  Qed.

  Definition scalar_restriction_functor
    : monoid_action_cat M' ⟶ monoid_action_cat M
    := make_functor _ scalar_restriction_is_functor.

End ScalarRestriction.

(** ** 11.1. Extension of scalars preserves monoid monoid action *)

  Section PreservesMonoidMonoidAction.

    Definition scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
      : monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M' → monoid_monoid_action M'
      := λ x, f (pr1 x) * pr2 x.

    
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
iscomprelfun (eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M))
  scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun

    
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
iscomprelfun (eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M))
  scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun

      
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
x, x': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hx: eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) x x'
scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
  x =
scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
  x'

      
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
x0, x'0: monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hx: eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) x0 x'0
x, x': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'

           y'' : monoid_monoid_action M
                 × monoid_monoid_action M')

                (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun

           scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
             x')
          (setproperty (monoid_monoid_action M')
             (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
                x)
             (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
                x')))),,
    (λ x : monoid_monoid_action M
           × monoid_monoid_action M',
     idpath
       (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
          x))),,
   ((λ (y
        y' : monoid_monoid_action M
             × monoid_monoid_action M')
     (Hy : make_hProp
             (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
                y =
              scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
                y')
             (setproperty (monoid_monoid_action M')
                (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
                   y)
                (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
                   y'))), ! Hy)
    :
    issymm
      (λ x
          x' : monoid_monoid_action M
               × monoid_monoid_action M',
       make_hProp
         (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
            x =
          scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
            x')
         (setproperty (monoid_monoid_action M')
            (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
               x)
            (scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
               x'))))) y y'

        
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
x, x': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hx: eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) x x'
y, y': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hy: hrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) y y'
H: ∑ a : M,
pr1 y' = action (pr1 y) a
× pr2 y = (f a + pr2 y')%addmonoid
scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_fun
  y' = (f (pr1 y) + (f (pr1 H) + pr2 y'))%addmonoid

        
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
x, x': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hx: eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) x x'
y, y': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hy: hrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) y y'
H: ∑ a : M,
pr1 y' = action (pr1 y) a
× pr2 y = (f a + pr2 y')%addmonoid
(f (action (pr1 y) (pr1 H)) + pr2 y')%addmonoid =
(f (pr1 y) + (f (pr1 H) + pr2 y'))%addmonoid

        
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
x, x': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hx: eqrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) x x'
y, y': monoid_monoid_action M × monoid_monoid_action M'
Hy: hrelation (monoid_monoid_action M) y y'
H: ∑ a : M,
pr1 y' = action (pr1 y) a
× pr2 y = (f a + pr2 y')%addmonoid
(f (pr1 y) + f (pr1 H) + pr2 y')%addmonoid =
(f (pr1 y) + (f (pr1 H) + pr2 y'))%addmonoid

        apply assocax.
    Qed.

    Definition scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor
      : (scalar_extension_functor (monoid_monoid_action M) : monoid_action M')
        → monoid_monoid_action M'
      := setquotuniv _ _ _ scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_mor_iscomprelfun.

    Definition scalar_extension_preserves_monoid_monoid_action_inv
      : monoid_monoid_action M'
        → (scalar_extension_functor (monoid_monoid_action M) : monoid_action M')
      := λ m, setquotpr _ (1 ,, m).

(** ** 11.2. Extension of scalars preserves the terminal *)

  Section PreservesTerminal.

    Context (terminal_element : M').

      : (scalar_extension_functor (terminal_monoid_action M) : monoid_action _)
        → (TerminalObject (terminal_monoid_action M') : monoid_action _)
      := λ x, tt.

      : (TerminalObject (terminal_monoid_action M') : monoid_action _)
        → (scalar_extension_functor (terminal_monoid_action M) : monoid_action _)
      := λ x, setquotpr _ (tt ,, terminal_element).

(** ** 11.3. Extension of scalars preserves binary products *)

  Section PreservesProduct.

    Context (terminal_element :
      ∏ (b1 b2 : M'),
      ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M), (b1 = f(a1) * c) × (b2 = f(a2) * c)).

    Context (element_is_terminal :
      ∏ (b1 b2 : M')
        (t := (terminal_element b1 b2))
        (t' : ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M), (b1 = f(a1) * c) × (b2 = f(a2) * c)),
        ∑ (a : M),
          (pr1 t) = f(a) * (pr1 t')
          × (pr12 t) * a = (pr12 t')
          × (pr122 t) * a = (pr122 t')).

    Section Isomorphism.

      Context (X X' : monoid_action M).

      Definition scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_mor_data
        (x : (X × X') × M')
        : (X × M') × X' × M'
        := (pr11 x ,, pr2 x) ,, (pr21 x ,, pr2 x).

      
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
terminal_element: ∏ b1 b2 : M',
∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× b2 = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
element_is_terminal: ∏ (b1 b2 : M')
(t := terminal_element b1 b2)
(t' : ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
      b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
      × b2 =
        (f a2 + c)%addmonoid),
∑ a : M,
pr1 t = (f a + pr1 t')%addmonoid
× (pr12 t + a)%addmonoid =
  pr12 t'
  × (pr122 t + a)%addmonoid =
    pr122 t'
X, X': monoid_action M
iscomprelrelfun
  (eqrelation (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M X X'))
  (eqreldirprod (eqrelation X) (eqrelation X'))
  scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_mor_data

      Qed.

      Definition scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_mor
        : setquot (eqrel_from_hrel (hrelation (action_binproduct_object X X'))) →
          setquot (eqrel_from_hrel (hrelation X)) × setquot (eqrel_from_hrel (hrelation X'))
        := funcomp
          (setquotfun _ _ _ scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_mor_iscomprelrelfun)
          (setquottodirprod (eqrelation X) (eqrelation X')).

      Definition scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data
        (x : (X × M') × X' × M')
        (t := terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x))
        : (X × X') × M'
        := ((
          action (pr11 x) (pr12 t) ,,
          action (pr12 x) (pr122 t)) ,,
          pr1 t).

terminal_element: ∏ b1 b2 : M',

× b2 = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid

(t := terminal_element b1 b2)
(t' : ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
      b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
      × b2 =
        (f a2 + c)%addmonoid),
∑ a : M,

× (pr12 t + a)%addmonoid =
  pr12 t'
  × (pr122 t + a)%addmonoid =
    pr122 t'
X, X': monoid_action M
x, x': (X × monoid_monoid_action M')
× X' × monoid_monoid_action M'
t:= terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x): ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
pr21 x = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× pr22 x = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
t':= terminal_element (pr21 x') (pr22 x'): ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
pr21 x' = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid

(∑ a : M,
 pr11 x' = action (pr11 x) a
 × pr21 x = (f a + pr21 x')%addmonoid)
→ (∑ a : M,
   pr12 x' = action (pr12 x) a
   × pr22 x = (f a + pr22 x')%addmonoid)
  → ∑ a : M,
    pr1 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x') =
    action
      (pr1
         (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x))
      a
    × pr2 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x) =
      (f a +
       pr2
         (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x'))%addmonoid

        
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
terminal_element: ∏ b1 b2 : M',
∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× b2 = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
element_is_terminal: ∏ (b1 b2 : M')
(t := terminal_element b1 b2)
(t' : ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
      b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
      × b2 =
        (f a2 + c)%addmonoid),
∑ a : M,
pr1 t = (f a + pr1 t')%addmonoid
× (pr12 t + a)%addmonoid =
  pr12 t'
  × (pr122 t + a)%addmonoid =
    pr122 t'
X, X': monoid_action M
x, x': (X × monoid_monoid_action M')
× X' × monoid_monoid_action M'
t:= terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x): ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
pr21 x = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× pr22 x = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
t':= terminal_element (pr21 x') (pr22 x'): ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
pr21 x' = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× pr22 x' = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
Hx1: ∑ a : M,
pr11 x' = action (pr11 x) a
× pr21 x = (f a + pr21 x')%addmonoid
Hx2: ∑ a : M,
pr12 x' = action (pr12 x) a
× pr22 x = (f a + pr22 x')%addmonoid
∑ a : M,
pr1 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x') =
action
  (pr1 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x)) a
× pr2 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x) =
  (f a +
   pr2 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x'))%addmonoid

        
M, M': monoid
f: monoidfun M M'
terminal_element: ∏ b1 b2 : M',
∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× b2 = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
element_is_terminal: ∏ (b1 b2 : M')
(t := terminal_element b1 b2)
(t' : ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
      b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
      × b2 =
        (f a2 + c)%addmonoid),
∑ a : M,
pr1 t = (f a + pr1 t')%addmonoid
× (pr12 t + a)%addmonoid =
  pr12 t'
  × (pr122 t + a)%addmonoid =
    pr122 t'
X, X': monoid_action M
x, x': (X × monoid_monoid_action M')
× X' × monoid_monoid_action M'
t:= terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x): ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
pr21 x = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× pr22 x = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
t':= terminal_element (pr21 x') (pr22 x'): ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
pr21 x' = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× pr22 x' = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
Hx1: ∑ a : M,
pr11 x' = action (pr11 x) a
× pr21 x = (f a + pr21 x')%addmonoid
Hx2: ∑ a : M,
pr12 x' = action (pr12 x) a
× pr22 x = (f a + pr22 x')%addmonoid
t'':= element_is_terminal 
  (pr21 x) (pr22 x)
  (pr1 t',,
   (pr1 Hx1 + pr12 t')%addmonoid,,
   (pr1 Hx2 + pr122 t')%addmonoid,,
   (pr22 Hx1 @
    maponpaths (op (f (pr1 Hx1)))
      (pr122 (pr2 t')) @
    ! assocax M' (f (pr1 Hx1)) 
        (f (pr12 t')) 
        (pr1 t') @
    ! maponpaths
        (λ x : M', (x + pr1 t')%addmonoid)
        (monoidfunmul f (pr1 Hx1) (pr12 t'))),,
   pr22 Hx2 @
   maponpaths (op (f (pr1 Hx2))) (pr222 (pr2 t')) @
   ! assocax M' (f (pr1 Hx2)) 
       (f (pr122 t')) 
       (pr1 t') @
   ! maponpaths
       (λ x : M', (x + pr1 t')%addmonoid)
       (monoidfunmul f (pr1 Hx2) (pr122 t'))): ∑ a : M,
pr1 (terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x)) =
(f a +
 pr1
   (pr1 t',,
    pr1 Hx1 + pr12 t',,
    pr1 Hx2 + pr122 t',,
    (pr22 Hx1 @
     maponpaths (op (f (pr1 Hx1)))
       (pr122 (pr2 t')) @
     ! assocax M' (f (pr1 Hx1)) 
         (f (pr12 t')) 
         (pr1 t') @
     ! maponpaths (λ x : M', x + pr1 t')
         (monoidfunmul f (pr1 Hx1) (pr12 t'))),,
    pr22 Hx2 @
    maponpaths (op (f (pr1 Hx2)))
      (pr222 (pr2 t')) @
    ! assocax M' (f (pr1 Hx2)) 
        (f (pr122 t')) 
        (pr1 t') @
    ! maponpaths (λ x : M', x + pr1 t')
        (monoidfunmul f (pr1 Hx2) (pr122 t'))))%addmonoid
× (pr12 (terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x)) + a)%addmonoid =
  pr12 (pr1 t',,
        (pr1 Hx1 + pr12 t')%addmonoid,,
        (pr1 Hx2 + pr122 t')%addmonoid,,
        (pr22 Hx1 @
         maponpaths 
           (op (f (pr1 Hx1))) 
           (pr122 (pr2 t')) @
         ! assocax M' 
             (f (pr1 Hx1)) 
             (f (pr12 t')) 
             (pr1 t') @
         ! maponpaths
             (λ x : M', (x + pr1 t')%addmonoid)
             (monoidfunmul f (pr1 Hx1) (pr12 t'))),,
        pr22 Hx2 @
        maponpaths 
          (op (f (pr1 Hx2))) 
          (pr222 (pr2 t')) @
        ! assocax M' 
            (f (pr1 Hx2)) 
            (f (pr122 t')) 
            (pr1 t') @
        ! maponpaths
            (λ x : M', (x + pr1 t')%addmonoid)
            (monoidfunmul f (pr1 Hx2) (pr122 t')))
  × (pr122 (terminal_element (pr21 x) (pr22 x)) +
     a)%addmonoid =
    pr122 (pr1 t',,
           (pr1 Hx1 + pr12 t')%addmonoid,,
           (pr1 Hx2 + pr122 t')%addmonoid,,
           (pr22 Hx1 @
            maponpaths 
              (op (f (pr1 Hx1)))
              (pr122 (pr2 t')) @
            ! assocax M' 
                (f (pr1 Hx1)) 
                (f (pr12 t')) 
                (pr1 t') @
            ! maponpaths
                (λ 
                 x : M', 
                 (x + pr1 t')%addmonoid)
                (monoidfunmul f 
                  (pr1 Hx1) 
                  (pr12 t'))),,
           pr22 Hx2 @
           maponpaths 
             (op (f (pr1 Hx2))) 
             (pr222 (pr2 t')) @
           ! assocax M' 
               (f (pr1 Hx2)) 
               (f (pr122 t')) 
               (pr1 t') @
           ! maponpaths
               (λ x : M', (x + pr1 t')%addmonoid)
               (monoidfunmul f 
                  (pr1 Hx2) 
                  (pr122 t')))
∑ a : M,
pr1 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x') =
action
  (pr1 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x)) a
× pr2 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x) =
  (f a +
   pr2 (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_data x'))%addmonoid

      Definition scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv
        : setquot (eqrel_from_hrel (hrelation X)) × setquot (eqrel_from_hrel (hrelation X')) →
          setquot (eqrel_from_hrel (hrelation (action_binproduct_object X X')))
        := funcomp
          (dirprodtosetquot (eqrelation X) (eqrelation X'))
          (setquotfun _ _ _ scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv_iscomprelrelfun).

terminal_element: ∏ b1 b2 : M',
∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
× b2 = (f a2 + c)%addmonoid
element_is_terminal: ∏ (b1 b2 : M')
(t := terminal_element b1 b2)
(t' : ∑ (c : M') (a1 a2 : M),
      b1 = (f a1 + c)%addmonoid
      × b2 =
        (f a2 + c)%addmonoid),
∑ a : M,
pr1 t = (f a + pr1 t')%addmonoid
× (pr12 t + a)%addmonoid =
  pr12 t'
  × (pr122 t + a)%addmonoid =
    pr122 t'

  (setquotinset
     (eqreldirprod 
        (eqrelation X) 
        (eqrelation X')))
  (setdirprod (setquotinset (eqrelation X))
     (setquotinset (eqrelation X')))
  (weqsetquottodirprod 
     (eqrelation X) 
     (eqrelation X')): z_iso
  (setquotinset
     (eqreldirprod 
        (eqrelation X) 
        (eqrelation X')))
  (setdirprod (setquotinset (eqrelation X))
     (setquotinset (eqrelation X')))

      Definition scalar_extension_binproduct_iso
        : z_iso
          (scalar_extension_functor (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M X X'))
          (binproducts_monoid_action_cat
            M'
            (scalar_extension_functor X)
            (scalar_extension_functor X'))
        := make_monoid_action_z_iso
          (scalar_extension_functor (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M X X'))
          (BinProductObject _ (binproducts_monoid_action_cat
            M'
            (scalar_extension_functor X)
            (scalar_extension_functor X')))
          (make_z_iso
            (C := HSET)
            (a := setquotinset _)
            (b := setdirprod (setquotinset _) (setquotinset _))
            scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_mor
            scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_inv
            scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_is_iso)
          scalar_extension_binproduct_iso_is_morphism.

    End Isomorphism.

Y, Y': monoid_action_cat M
isBinProduct (monoid_action_cat M')
  (scalar_extension_functor Y)
  (scalar_extension_functor Y')
  (scalar_extension_functor
     (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M Y Y'))
  (# scalar_extension_functor
     (BinProductPr1 (monoid_action_cat M)
        (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M Y Y')))
  (# scalar_extension_functor
     (BinProductPr2 (monoid_action_cat M)
        (binproducts_monoid_action_cat M Y Y')))

        use (isBinProduct_eq_arrow _ _
          (iso_to_isBinProduct _ _ (z_iso_to_iso (scalar_extension_binproduct_iso Y Y'))));
        abstract now (
          apply monoid_action_morphism_eq;
          intro;
          use (issurjsetquotpr _ x (_ ,, isasetsetquot _ _ _) _);
          intro y;
          rewrite <- (pr2 y)
        ).
    Defined.

  End PreservesProduct.

End ScalarExtension.
